Ottos bluesy, muscular voice and dynamic stage presence earned him the respect of industry gatekeepers and the adoration of legions of country music fans. However, theres more to life than chart success and constant touring. Real country music is fed by life experience and Otto stepped away from the spotlight to focus on family and pour his life into a new season of songwriting. Now hes returned to recording with an infectious new single, Somewhere Tonight, that reveals a renewed commitment to creating his own unique brand of country music. During his self-imposed hiatus, Otto penned hundreds of songs, but he says when he co-wrote Somewhere Tonight, he knew there was something special, and when he began performing it in his shows, that hunch was confirmed. Otto has always had an uncanny ability to write songs that give voice to the hopes, dreams and simple desires of his audience. Its a gift he began developing early in life. Otto has never been in a better place. He has a happy home life and creatively hes on fire. Hes writing, touring, producing other new artists and working on a new album.
